  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText12067335538797582246" style="display:none"><i>Librarian's Note: The ISBN 9789383260195 for this book was also used by "<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25636238.Shekhar_Kapur_s_Devi___Vol__1" title="Shekhar Kapur's Devi - Vol. 1" rel="nofollow noopener">Shekhar Kapur's Devi - Vol. 1</a>" by Samit Basu.</i><br /><br /><b>There are two sides to every love story. Now hear Will’s.</b><br /><br /><i>Colleen Hoover’s New York Times bestselling Slammed series has brought countless readers to their knees with a whirlwind of love, passion, and heartache. </i><br /><br />Layken and Will’s love has managed to withstand the toughest of circumstances and the young lovers, now married, are beginning to feel safe and secure in their union. As much as Layken relishes their new life together, she finds herself wanting to know everything there is to know about her husband, even though Will makes it clear he prefers to keep the painful memories of the past where they belong. Still, he can’t resist his wife’s pleas and so he begins to untangle his side of the story, revealing for the first time his most intimate feelings and thoughts, retelling both the good and bad moments, and sharing a few shocking confessions of his own from the time when they first met.<br /><br />In <i>This Girl</i>, Will tells the story of their complicated relationship from <i>his </i>point of view. Their future rests on how well they deal with the past in this final installment of the beloved Slammed<i> </i>series.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer439810273" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17985110207083555346"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395184i/761043._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395184ra/761044.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> <u> THIS IS ME SHOUTING FROM THE ROOFTOPS </u> !!!!!! <br/>THIS. BOOK. IS. PHENOMENAL.<br/>I'm laughing. I'm crying. I'm shaking. <br/>It was perfect. Every single line was perfect. <br/>Beautiful. Heartbreak. Breathtaking. <br/>Unputdownable.<br/>Pure. butterflying. gold. <br/><br/>6 HUGE STARS!!! </b><br/><br/>Books like this are the reason why I love reading.<br/><br/>Colleen Hoover has outdone herself. She managed to take a story that we love and retell it from the hero’s POV while still making every single word of it feel new, fresh and powerful.<br/><br/>Yes, technica</span>
  <span id="freeText17985110207083555346" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395184i/761043._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395184ra/761044.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> <u> THIS IS ME SHOUTING FROM THE ROOFTOPS </u> !!!!!! <br>THIS. BOOK. IS. PHENOMENAL.<br>I'm laughing. I'm crying. I'm shaking. <br>It was perfect. Every single line was perfect. <br>Beautiful. Heartbreak. Breathtaking. <br>Unputdownable.<br>Pure. butterflying. gold. <br><br>6 HUGE STARS!!! </b><br><br>Books like this are the reason why I love reading.<br><br>Colleen Hoover has outdone herself. She managed to take a story that we love and retell it from the hero’s POV while still making every single word of it feel new, fresh and powerful.<br><br>Yes, technically it’s a retelling of Slammed from Will’s POV but there is SO much more. There are new scenes, added story lines, and even a epilogue that is guaranteed to make your heart squeeze. Not one word of it felt repetitive.<br><br>Reading this book was like taking a beautiful walk down memory lane. It’s been over a year since I read Slammed and Point of Retreat. Those two books are one of the reasons I started blogging. Slammed was actually the first book ever that inspired me to write anything about it. At the time, it was only a small review paragraph where I tried to convey my love for the story but it was something. The depth to which those books hit me was unlike any other book I’d read at that point. I “felt” the story with every single part of my heart and soul.<br><br>But before starting This Girl, I didn’t have time to reread either of them and I wondered if I’d be able to connect to it as strongly as I did to the first two. But can I just say that barely 10 lines into the book, every, <u> single</u> emotion that the original books had instilled in me came flooding back. My heart clenched. My throat closed up. I was right back there. Right. There. In this beautifully crafted world, surrounded by the characters I’d come to love with my whole heart.<br><br>There is something simply <u> magical</u> about reading a book that revisits characters you are already in love with. EVERYTHING just has so much more weight. It’s like the best possible kind of reunion imaginable.<br><br>Do you need to re-read Slammed and Point of Retreat before reading this? No. But you do need to read them at least once first? For sure!<br><br>Without spoilers, I want to tell you a little about this book. The whole book is from Will’s POV. I know it’s being called “Slammed from Will’s POV” but it is <u> so </u> much <u> more </u>. It actually takes place after Point of Retreat and is a continuation of their story in that respect. But, a major part of the book, is Lake asking Will what his perspective was on a lot of the things they went through together, and asking him things about himself that neither she nor us (the readers) knew.<br><br>And because when you read this, you’ll already know the general story, something as simple as this line can just make your breath catch:<br><br><blockquote> <i> “I cross the street, unable to take my eyes off the girl in the U-Haul.” </i>
</blockquote> <br>And then, finally, after the alternate story of Slammed has been caught up, Will and Lake’s story progresses even farther ((cue the squeeling)) including an absolutely perfect, utterly beautiful, heartwarming epilogue that literally left me smiling, crying and shaking.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “She doesn’t speak, but she doesn’t have to. I know in these moments when it’s just her and me and nothing else, that she truly, soul-deep, loves me.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>I could NOT put this book down. It was riveting, captivating, and I was so wrapped up in the story that I didn’t even notice that I literally read until the sun came up. I wanted both to rush through it and yet also to read it as slow as possible to savor every and every world. It absolutely consumed me.<br><br>This book was perfect from start to finish. It captured that heart-fluttering power of first love told from the POV of one of our favorite book heroes. Everything was just so emotionally charged – the flirting, the introduction, the crushing, the chemistry, the sheer, raw, passionate intensity that just rolled off the page. Like I said, perfect!<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “I can’t remember feeling this way since… well, ever. It’s new. It’s scary. It’s exciting. It’s nerve-wracking. It’s calming. It’s every single emotion I’ve ever felt balled up into an intense urge to grab a hold of her and never let go.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>There are also new slams!! A few of them actually. And ohhhhh my are they ever beautiful! You know, I’ve never been into poetry, for some reason I just can’t seem to get into it, but the slams in this series are just so POWERFUL that you can’t help but “feel” them.<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395184i/761045._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For those of you who have yet to start this series, you should know that there is a reason that Colleen Hoover is getting the acclaim she’s receiving right now. Everything about her writing – the story, the style, the characters, is simply breathtaking. The level of EMOTION that exists in nearly every line of this book is just overwhelming. I loved every minute. Her words speak straight to your soul.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “I suddenly don’t care where we are or who might be watching us. I have to kiss her. I have to.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br><br>I laughed, I cried, and sometimes I laughed through my tears. And when the FULL understanding of the title hit me, I can’t even describe to you what I felt. Just. WOW.<br><br>My 6-star book list is reserved for those few books that, from start to finish, go above and beyond. That grab a hold of my heart so strongly that a year later, I can just pick the books up and the emotions are right THERE. That tell a story that is so beautiful, real, original, and powerful that it leaves a mark on my heart that I know will be there for ever.<br><br>This book did that.<br><br>Soul deep, guys.<br><br>Just, butterflying perfect.<br><br>6 huge stars.<br><br><i> I received an ARC review copy directly from the author in exchange for an honest review. </i><br><br>Here's how I see Will:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395184i/761046.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17985110207083555346" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer396505948" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8613839199829075264"><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/af255582-6253-40ab-9d61-244f7dcab714_zps3a78fd80.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748894.jpg' alt=' photo af255582-6253-40ab-9d61-244f7dcab714_zps3a78fd80.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I love Slammed and Point of Retreat. Seriously loved them... but this, this was something else entirely. Love is not a strong enough word about how I feel about this book! Colleen Hoover’s writing is beautiful, magical, wonderful. This was essentially Slammed, from Will Cooper’s perspective, but it was so much more than that! Will and Lake are <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[on their honeymoon <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and talking about the past... She is asking him questions and we are getting to see all of our favor</span>
  <span id="freeText8613839199829075264" style="display:none"><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/af255582-6253-40ab-9d61-244f7dcab714_zps3a78fd80.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748894.jpg" alt=" photo af255582-6253-40ab-9d61-244f7dcab714_zps3a78fd80.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I love Slammed and Point of Retreat. Seriously loved them... but this, this was something else entirely. Love is not a strong enough word about how I feel about this book! Colleen Hoover’s writing is beautiful, magical, wonderful. This was essentially Slammed, from Will Cooper’s perspective, but it was so much more than that! Will and Lake are <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[on their honeymoon <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and talking about the past... She is asking him questions and we are getting to see all of our favorite scenes through his eyes. If you haven't read Slammed or Point of Retreat, you should do that RIGHT NOW! This review won’t be a normal one... I may just spend it gushing about all things Will Cooper and tell you how much I loved this book, but thats okay, right?<br><i>
  <blockquote>I met this <b>guy</b> last year<br>I was reading this book called <b>Slammed</b><br>and it just spoke to me.<br><b>Will Cooper</b> is not my normal book boyfriend...<br>He’s <b>sweet, caring, and all kinds of WONDERFUL</b><br>I fell for him. <br>And now I get his side of the <b>story</b>
</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/e152e321-1edc-4138-bbe4-f84d63119e63_zps0a0c698e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748895._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo e152e321-1edc-4138-bbe4-f84d63119e63_zps0a0c698e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>You need a few reasons why I love Will Cooper... Well, he pretty much speaks for himself:<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> Out of all the reasons I can come up with for her to go, there is only one reason I can come up with for her to stay. I love her.<br><br>She deserves to be kissed by someone who loves her. Someone who spends every waking moment trying to do everything right by her. Someone who would rather die than see her hurt. She doesn't deserve to be kissed by anyone other than me.<br><br>“Layken Cooper, I love you. I’ve loved you since the second I laid eyes on you and I haven’t stopped loving you for a second since.”<br><br>“This is it, Lake.” I say, both pointing back and forth between us. “It’s real now. I’m not walking away from you again. Ever.”<br><br>“You want to know my sweet?” I ask her. She nods. I kiss her on the forehead. “You. Always you.”<br><br>“Wife,” I say, staring straight into her eyes. “Think what you want, but there isn’t a single woman in this whole damn universe that I could ever love like I love you.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Can you say SWOON??? I think Will Cooper is the most swoonworthy book boy out there! And he writes poetry...<br><i>
  <blockquote>I dreamt about this girl last night. <br><b>Wow</b>. This <b>girl. </b><br>This girl completely shatters the window to my soul and crawls inside. </blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/190b91b5-008d-4b91-a13b-87608ee45653_zps53cda14f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748896.jpg" alt=" photo 190b91b5-008d-4b91-a13b-87608ee45653_zps53cda14f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/e9ccb0fe-aaaa-4411-919a-e283bcf6c013_zps4b5c74cd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748897.jpg" alt=" photo e9ccb0fe-aaaa-4411-919a-e283bcf6c013_zps4b5c74cd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book was perfection from start to finish. And that ending... the epilogue had me crying happy tears! <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <b>
    <i> “You, baby girl. You’re my final piece.” </i>
  </b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>This series is a MUST READ in my book! <br><br>Now I will leave you with some of my FAVORITE things about this series...<br><br><b>Will and Layken in the laundry room...</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/7aaf225a-7305-4db9-8a5c-a7c170e70664_zpsce768e81.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748898.jpg" alt=" photo 7aaf225a-7305-4db9-8a5c-a7c170e70664_zpsce768e81.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>The Avett Brother’s and Slam Poetry</b><br><i>And that’s when it happens... the most beautiful sound in the world. Sure, the song is beautiful, all Avett brother’s songs are beautiful. But the sound I’m hearing is the sound of commonality. The sound of similarity.</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/d3ffef60-14f6-4f27-a4dd-beb55000a953_zps5937ea06.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748899.jpg" alt=" photo d3ffef60-14f6-4f27-a4dd-beb55000a953_zps5937ea06.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/eb38c6a9-d01c-4ef2-b6f0-a96814d306b9_zps83c827d3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748900.jpg" alt=" photo eb38c6a9-d01c-4ef2-b6f0-a96814d306b9_zps83c827d3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/THISGIRL-Slam_zps892ac474.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748901.jpg" alt=" photo THISGIRL-Slam_zps892ac474.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Will and Lake’s first date</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/THISGIRL-chocolatemilk_zpsd56a131e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748902.jpg" alt=" photo THISGIRL-chocolatemilk_zpsd56a131e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> SUCK AND SWEET!</b><br><i>
  <blockquote>“She rolls her eyes. 'Will, this date is going to be my <b>suck</b> for the day if you don't become a little more talkative.'<br>I laugh. 'Yes, we're going to Club N9NE. Yes, we're going to dinner first. Yes, I wrote a slam for you. Yes, we're leaving the club early so we can go back to my house and hardcore make out in the dark.'<br>'You just became my <b>sweet</b>,' she says.” </blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/THISGIRL-suck_zpsadb85ff5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748903.jpg" alt=" photo THISGIRL-suck_zpsadb85ff5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/9cd8f315-1d66-4b29-ae5f-b91850b0784d_zpsa903797a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748904.jpg" alt=" photo 9cd8f315-1d66-4b29-ae5f-b91850b0784d_zpsa903797a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Pumpkin Carving</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/aa593ebc-7165-4347-abd5-a08d0d97c573_zpsd749ecf6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748905.jpg" alt=" photo aa593ebc-7165-4347-abd5-a08d0d97c573_zpsd749ecf6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Butterfly ;D</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/512a665e-f678-4745-bf05-228c87d51e20_zpsb07e0ae4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748906.jpg" alt=" photo 512a665e-f678-4745-bf05-228c87d51e20_zpsb07e0ae4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Lake’s mom’s advice to her</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/THISGIRL-3things_zps9f536313.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748907.jpg" alt=" photo THISGIRL-3things_zps9f536313.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Will and Lake’s journey....</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/a9ad2b88-e67a-4ed7-871b-57dead41eec1_zps0573a234.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388404i/748908._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo a9ad2b88-e67a-4ed7-871b-57dead41eec1_zps0573a234.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I know this wasn’t so much a review, more like an excited rant, but Colleen Hoover’s books do this to me! <br><br>This book deserves more than 5 stars...<br><br>Read it and love it! &lt;3</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8613839199829075264" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_470341812" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/470341812" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/470341812?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2013-release">2013-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=unputdownable">unputdownable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=tearjerkers">tearjerkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer470341812" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4842647744701077000"><b>5+++++ BUTTERFLYING AMAZING STARS. ❤</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399786i/774024.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399786ra/774025.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><br/><b>COLLEEN.HOOVER.NEVER.DISAPPOINTS.</b> And once again, she has proven this statement right. <b>This Girl</b> was the perfect final chapter to a magnificent series that will forever reside on my all time favorites shelf. This story was so beautifully written that I almost wanted to highlight the entire book. And well, reading the story from Will's POV surely provided a lot of *swoon* and *sigh* worthy moments...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399786i/774026.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>But I'll go ahead and reveal it to you anyway...</i><br/><br/><i>
  <b>This Gi</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText4842647744701077000" style="display:none"><b>5+++++ BUTTERFLYING AMAZING STARS. ❤</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399786i/774024.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399786ra/774025.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><b>COLLEEN.HOOVER.NEVER.DISAPPOINTS.</b> And once again, she has proven this statement right. <b>This Girl</b> was the perfect final chapter to a magnificent series that will forever reside on my all time favorites shelf. This story was so beautifully written that I almost wanted to highlight the entire book. And well, reading the story from Will's POV surely provided a lot of *swoon* and *sigh* worthy moments...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399786i/774026.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>But I'll go ahead and reveal it to you anyway...</i><br><br><i>
  <b>This Girl</b>
</i> is the third and final installment in the Slammeds-series by Colleen Hoover and just like the first two books, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13372690.Slammed__Slammed___1_" title="Slammed (Slammed, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Slammed</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13496084.Point_of_Retreat__Slammed___2_" title="Point of Retreat (Slammed, #2) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Point of Retreat</a>, I have LOVED every single moment of reading this book. Every story has two sides and in this final part of the series, we finally hear Will's side of the story...<br><br><b>Will --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399786i/774027.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Layken --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399786i/774028.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399786i/774029.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Let me tell you something about this book...<br><br><b>This book</b> is the kind of book that will make you <b>laugh</b>,<br>It will make you <b>cry</b>,<br>It will make you <b>swoon</b>,<br>It will make your <b>heart skip a beat</b>,<br>It's the kind of book that will stay with you <b>forever</b>.<br><br><b>This book</b> made me <b>remember</b><br>Why I love <b>reading</b> so much.<br>Spending time with all these <b>special and unique characters</b><br>Made me <b>forget</b> about the rest of the world for a while.<br>It made me happy to just be in this <b>own private world</b>.<br><br>A world filled with two people in love like <b>Will and Lake</b>,<br>With inspiring mothers like <b>Julia</b>,<br>With supportive best friends like <b>Eddie and Gavin</b>,<br>With amazing kids like <b>Caulder and Kell</b>,<br>A world where all of them try to <b>make the best out of the life they're given.</b><br><br>There are so many things I'll forever remember about this series;<br>The beautiful <b>slams</b>,<br>The inspiring music of <b>The Avett Brothers</b>,<br>The funny <b>Suck and Sweet time-moments</b>,<br>Kell and his <b>backwards talking</b>. The list is endless...<br><br>But what I'll remember most of all,<br>Is how this series made me <b>feel</b>,<br>How it <b>schooled</b> me about <b>love, life and friendship</b>,<br>But mostly about the <b>power of words</b><br>With this <b>final piece</b> that binds all the loose ends <b>together, forever</b>.</i><br><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br><br>In <i>This Girl</i> <b>Will</b> tells us the story of how he and Layken first meet, and how they fell <b>seriously, deeply, madly, incredibly, and undeniably</b> in <b>love</b>...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399786i/774030.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399786i/774031.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Then this girl completely shatters the windows to my soul and climb inside."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>It wasn't always an easy story to read, we don't only get to re-live the beautiful, joyous moments, but also the sad, heartbreaking ones...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399786i/774032.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Responsibilities and heartbreak are what keeps these two apart.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i><b>Death</b>. The only thing inevitable in <b>life</b>.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>But, eventually they realize they need to put the <i>
  <b>emphasis</b>
</i> back on <i>
  <b>life</b>
</i> and that together, they can overcome whatever difficulties life may throw their way. Because that's what life sometimes does; it gets all up in <b>their way</b>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I've never been so consumed by the thought of someone in my entire life. This is the last thing I need right now, but somehow it's the only thing I want."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399786ra/774033.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399786i/774034.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At the same time, this story also gives us a glimpse of the future Will and Lake share. It constantly switches from the present to the past, allowing us a complete view of Will and Lake's story. Colleen Hoover really ties all the loose ends together and manages to wrap the story together in the most beautiful way possible. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>"You, baby girl, you're my final piece." &lt;3</b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br></p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399786ra/774035.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
</p><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"She deserves to be kissed by someone who loves her. Someone who spends every waking moment trying to do everything right by her. Someone who would rather die than see her hurt. She doesn't deserve to be kissed by anyone other than me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399786i/774036.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It was a true pleasure reading Will's side of the story. I already LOVED him in Slammed and Point of Retreat, but reading all of the events from his point of view made me love him even more. He's by far, one of my favorite male lead characters EVER. And the new slam he wrote? BREATHTAKING.<br><br>But my favorite is still ❤ <b>The Lake</b> ❤<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386353i/745815.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>What it comes down to is this:</i><b> I BUTTERFLYING LOVE EVERYTHING ABOUT THIS SERIES.</b> And if you haven't read it yet, go ahead and READ IT. And then, come tell me about how much you loved it, okay? Okay. There's so much more I would want to say about these books, but I don't want to spoil it for anyone who hasn't read it yet. So I'll leave you with this last quote (by another one of my favorite authors, John Green); which to me applies perfectly to this series:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399786i/774037._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>This series falls into that category...</i> Filled with <b>beautiful, heartwarming, funny, sweet, unforgettable and EPIC moments</b>, this series falls in a category of its own. And <b>This Girl</b> was the <b>PERFECT</b> ending to this <b>FANTASTIC</b> series. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Let's not fall apart again," I whisper. She looks me in the eyes. "Never."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399786i/774038.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>"You want to know my sweet?" I ask her.<br><br>She nods.<br><br>I kiss her on the forehead. "You. Always you."</i>
</b><br><br><br><b>&lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3</b><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="4842647744701077000" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_383636225" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/383636225" />
    <a title="Jess (the cozy reader)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6688090-jess-the-cozy-reader"><img alt="Jess (the cozy reader)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589164982p2/6688090.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/383636225?book_show_action=true">Aug 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jess (the cozy reader)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jess (the cozy reader)" href="/user/show/6688090-jess-the-cozy-reader">Jess (the cozy reader)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688090-jess-the-cozy-reader?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688090-jess-the-cozy-reader?shelf=sigh-happy-books">sigh-happy-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688090-jess-the-cozy-reader?shelf=great-contemporary-romance">great-contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer383636225" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2127828410392134093">Every time I read Colleen Hoover's books, I am left speechless, emotionally attached, and not wanting to let go. Will, Lake, and the rest of the of the gang in the Slammed Series have made permanent residency in my heart. So even though it was bittersweet to say goodbye, I couldn't be happier with how Colleen has ended Will and Lake's story. It left me with, forgive the pun, "butterflies" and happy tears.<br/><br/>I can never get enough of Will Cooper, and reading this book has only made me fall even hard</span>
  <span id="freeText2127828410392134093" style="display:none">Every time I read Colleen Hoover's books, I am left speechless, emotionally attached, and not wanting to let go. Will, Lake, and the rest of the of the gang in the Slammed Series have made permanent residency in my heart. So even though it was bittersweet to say goodbye, I couldn't be happier with how Colleen has ended Will and Lake's story. It left me with, forgive the pun, "butterflies" and happy tears.<br><br>I can never get enough of Will Cooper, and reading this book has only made me fall even harder for the man. Seriously, why can't he be real? I loved getting the flashback glimpses from Slammed, but in a whole new light from Will's perspective. All those moments from the first novel that made me think, what was going on in that boy's head? Well they were definitely answered, and let me just say that I love Will Cooper's mind.<br><br>Now for my absolute favorite parts. The wonderful epilogue, and Will's last poem: My Final Piece! I can't tell you how many times I have gone back to re-read it (plenty, I assure you). It makes me so darn happy, and it closes the series perfectly.<br><br>I cannot thank Colleen enough for making this story come to life. She is the Wonder Woman of the book world, and for many years to come!<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/glee%20clapping" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/377398.gif" alt="glee clapping photo: Emma and Rachel clapping smitten.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="2127828410392134093" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_603154819" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/603154819" />
    <a title="Rose" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3399699-rose"><img alt="Rose" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1386022874p2/3399699.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/603154819?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rose" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rose" href="/user/show/3399699-rose">Rose</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=realistic-fiction">realistic-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=zero-stars-is-too-much-for-this">zero-stars-is-too-much-for-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=arc-or-galley">arc-or-galley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer603154819" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16635579553662528451">There's a part of me that debated writing a review for this book at all considering the majority of this is just rehashed material from the first book with little new offerings. How do you write a review on a book in which the majority just copy/pasted material with some reworkings from a different perspective character of another novel? It's one thing if maybe it was a novella telling some slightly different perspective points but still offering new insights, or if it were a short story capturi</span>
  <span id="freeText16635579553662528451" style="display:none">There's a part of me that debated writing a review for this book at all considering the majority of this is just rehashed material from the first book with little new offerings. How do you write a review on a book in which the majority just copy/pasted material with some reworkings from a different perspective character of another novel? It's one thing if maybe it was a novella telling some slightly different perspective points but still offering new insights, or if it were a short story capturing a single segment in time - which were both alternatives Hoover could've perused if she wanted to continue with Will's perspective point, I think. I have no doubt that would've been something I picked up, even if I didn't care so much for the first two books in this series. With "Slammed", while I didn't care for the story, I still appreciated what it offered and I understood why people liked the story - I just expected more from it. "Point of Retreat" was shaky because Will's voice didn't sound like an authentic male voice to me and much of it was one point of drama and odd events to the next.<br /><br />But this? <b>This was lazy.</b> I hate saying it, or saying something about anyone else's writing which various people can find value even with its qualms, but I think someone has to. I'm being about as blunt and honest about it as I can be.<br /><br />This was a lazy effort and not worth the time taken to read. I'm extremely disappointed in reading "This Girl". I know Hoover can do a better work than this and this feels like it was just released to ride on the coattails of popularity this series has spawned. There's very little, if anything truly *new* about this book, and the material that is considered new? Not worth the retracing. Apart from honeymoon scenes where Lake and Will retread over their meeting and coming to terms with each other, this had very little weight to it. Some new poems and some intermittent sex scenes do not make for a compelling story. I'm sorry, it just doesn't at all. Lake doesn't show much growth (after all, she gets jealous and angry over things that happened in the PAST and are being retold to her when she practically begs Will to tell her anyway - and that's taken for an actual point of substantiated conflict. Really?!). And for a perspective character, Will's narration is extremely whiny, lust heavy, and NOT an authentic male voice. At all. I think it's safe to say that with this third book written in a male voice in Hoover's bibliography, her weakness is writing from male character perspectives. <br /><br />If I wanted to pick up reading "Slammed" again, I - among many other readers - probably would've had no qualms about doing so and letting Will's thoughts be left in mystery (part of the beauty of a piece of writing is letting some stuff be to the reader's imagination) - much of it is implied in the first book, it didn't need a retracing. This didn't feel like a full enough story to be retold in the way it was and it was just a waste of time having to backtrack through all of that just to cherry pick whatever new experiences Will had to offer in the narrative. It was tedious and a chore to read, probably even moreso than my recent reading of "Losing Hope" - which is a retelling of Hoover's hero Holder from the "Hopeless" series. I would actually give Hoover credit for attempting to develop Holder the way she did in that, because in comparison, "This Girl" didn't do anything at all to expand upon Will's character or any of the other characters it presented - the side characters were threadbare at best.<br /><br />I don't know if I can say more than that, really. It was a quick read for me, because much of this I already knew - been there, done that, deja vu. It's not worth my time or money to spend on something that's does nothing to expand on a story that's already been told, and I have to be firm on that. And I'm sure there are others - even fans of the first two books - who would feel the same way and be just as disappointed in this effort.<br /><br />Not recommended.<br /><br />Overall score: 0 stars.<br /><br />Note: I received this as an ARC from NetGalley, from the publisher Atria Books.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16635579553662528451" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Dd" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9444787-dd"><img alt="Dd" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/637945673?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer637945673" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17577987638762626292"><br/><b>
  <i>This review is very long<br/>So long, in fact, that your attention span<br/>May be stretched to its very limits<br/>But that’s okay.</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>This Girl<br/><br/><br/>This couple<br/><br/><br/>And their Love Story....</i><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>....took my breath away!!!</i>
</b><br/><br/>----------------------------------------------------------<br/><br/>Hello Readers,<br/><br/>So what do I tell you about <b>this book</b>?<br/><br/><br/><b>Well, let me start with a story....</b><br/><br/>A girl once moved into a new town, far, far away from where she used to live.Along with her were her mother and her little brother.<br/><br/><b>This girl</b> was tough.Resilient</span>
  <span id="freeText17577987638762626292" style="display:none"><br /><b>
  <i>This review is very long<br />So long, in fact, that your attention span<br />May be stretched to its very limits<br />But that’s okay.</i>
</b><br /><br /><i>This Girl<br /><br /><br />This couple<br /><br /><br />And their Love Story....</i><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>....took my breath away!!!</i>
</b><br /><br />----------------------------------------------------------<br /><br />Hello Readers,<br /><br />So what do I tell you about <b>this book</b>?<br /><br /><br /><b>Well, let me start with a story....</b><br /><br />A girl once moved into a new town, far, far away from where she used to live.Along with her were her mother and her little brother.<br /><br /><b>This girl</b> was tough.Resilient.Though she had lost her mentor, her guide, her hero, all wrapped up in one and only.... her father, she moved on <b>with all her strength wrapped up in a smile.</b><br /><br /><br /><i>This girl was Layken.</i><br /><br /><br /><br />And then she met with the boy-next-door who lived with his young brother.<b>This boy</b> was tall, polite, and just plain hot.<br /><br /><br /><i>This boy was Will.</i><br /><br /><br />And then <b>this boy</b> swept <b>this girl</b> off her feet.He asked her out on a date to begin <b>their</b> story.<br /><br /><br /><i>Hmmm...but don't they always? Seemed like the Princess got her Prince Charming.And what would happen next, was really not very difficult to guess.</i><br /><br /><br /><b>Did you then? Guess...I mean.</b><br /><br /><br /><i>Well I couldn't.</i><br /><br /><br />Because what happened next was <b>surprising</b>, <b>amazing</b>, <b>breathtaking</b>, <b>powerful</b>, <b>raw</b>, <b>stunning</b>, and the rest was.....<br /><br /><br />.....<b>butterflying history</b>.<br /><br />--------------------------------------------------------<br /><br />But it was still <b>incomplete</b>.I still hungered for more.I couldn't really pinpoint it, but something was missing.<br /><br />And that something was Will's thoughts, his feelings, his hopes, his fears about....<b>this girl.</b><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Readers, this book is a wonderful collage.A collage of memories present and past.</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />---------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Their honeymoon--</i>
</b><br /><br /><i>IF I TOOK every romantic poem, every book, every song, and every movie I’ve ever read, heard, or seen and extracted the breathtaking moments, somehow bottling them up, they would pale in comparison to this moment.<br /><br />This moment is incomparable.</i><br /><br /><br />-----------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><br /><i>From this point on I’ll be able to do that for her.<br />Should there be any more burdens I’ll be able to carry them for her. It’s all I’ve ever wanted to do for<br />this girl since the moment I first laid eyes on her.</i><br /><br /><br />------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>His break-up with Vaughn--</i>
</b><br /><br /><i>“Will, don’t,” she pleads. “Please don’t be mad at me.” She’s looking up at me with tears in her eyes. When she cries, her eyes turn a glossy, deep shade of blue.I used to tell her they were the exact same color as the <b>ocean</b>. Looking into her eyes right now almost makes me despise the ocean.</i><br /><br /><br />------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>First meeting with Layken--</i>
</b><br /><br /><i>Wow. Those eyes. They’re the most incredible shade of green I’ve ever seen. I try to compare the color to something, but nothing comes to mind. It’s so unique, it’s like her eyes have just invented their own hue.</i><br /><br /><b>This girl became his Lake.</b><br /><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>So you <b>keep</b> your <b>ocean</b>,<br /><b>I’ll</b> take the <b>Lake</b>.</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />----------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Their first date</i>
</b>--<br /><br /><i>“And what’s a slam?”<br /><br />I pause for a second and smile at her. “It’s poetry,” I say. “It’s what I’m all about.” I wait for the laughter, but it doesn’t come.</i><br /><br /><br /><b>And then came his whole life, condensed into a one-minute poem.</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Death. The only thing inevitable in <b>life.</b></i>
</blockquote><br />But even after he laid his life bare for her to see....<br /><br /><br /><i>When I look into her eyes, it’s not pity I see at all.She’s still looking at me with hope in her eyes.<br /><br />This girl just became privy to everything I’ve been scared to tell her about my life. The death of my parents, the anger I held toward them, the amount of responsibility I now face, the fact that I’m all Caulder has—and she’s still looking at me with hope in her tear-filled eyes.</i><br /><br /><br /><b>Yes, this girl, this girl changed his life.</b><br /><br /><br />But...we already know, the real challenges came after that.The greatest of hurdles came after that.<br /><br /><br /><b>So listen as <b>this boy</b> recounts to <b>this girl</b>..... <b>their</b> story.</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>I dreamt about this girl last night.<br /><b>Wow.</b><br />This <b>girl.</b><br />In my <b>dream</b> I was standing on the edge of a <b>cliff</b><br />Looking <b>down</b> over a <b>vast, barren valley below</b><br />I wasn’t wearing any <b>shoes</b> and the rocks were <b>crumbling</b> beneath my <b>toes.</b><br />It would have been so <b>easy</b> to take a step back,<br />To <b>move</b> away from the <b>ledge,</b><br />Away from a <b>certain inevitable life</b> that had <b>somehow</b> been <b>determined</b> for me<br />A life that had <b>somehow</b> become my only option.<br />It had been my life for <b>two years</b> and I accepted that.<br />I had not <b>embraced</b> it,<br />But I had <b>accepted</b> it.<br />It was where I belonged.<br />As much as it didn’t <b>appeal</b> to me, as much as I <b>yearned</b> for the <b>rivers</b> and <b>mountains</b> and <b>trees</b>,<br />As much as I <b>yearned</b> to hear their <b>songs</b> . . .<br />To hear their . . . <b>poetry</b>?<br />It was apparent that what <b>I</b> yearned for<br />wasn’t <b>decided</b> by me . . .<br />it was decided <b>for</b> me.<br />So . . . I did the only thing I could do.<br />The only thing I <b>should</b> do.<br />I prepared myself to <b>embrace</b> this life.<br />I sucked it up and took a <b>deep</b> breath. I placed my <b>hands</b> on the edge of the <b>cliff</b> and began to <b>lower</b> myself onto the <b>rocks</b> protruding from the <b>edge</b>. I <b>burrowed</b> my <b>fingers deep</b> into the<br /><b>crevices</b> and <b>slowly</b> began lowering myself <b>down.</b><br />Down into the <b>vast,<br />barren<br />valley</b><br />that had become<br />my<br /><b>life</b>.<br />But <b>then</b> . . .<br />Then this <b>girl</b> . . .<br />Holy <b>hell</b>, this <b>girl</b> . . .<br />She appeared out of <b>nowhere</b>, standing <b>directly</b> in front of me on the edge of that <b>cliff</b>. She<br />looked <b>down</b> at me with her <b>sad eyes</b> that ran a <b>million</b> miles <b>deep</b> . . .<br />and she <b>smiled</b> at me.<br />This girl <b>smiled</b> at me.<br />A <b>look</b> that cut <b>straight</b> to my core and <b>pierced</b> through my <b>heart</b> like a <b>million</b> of Cupid’s<br />arrows,<br /><b>One</b> right on top of the <b>other</b>, on top of the <b>other</b>, on top of the <b>other</b><br /><b>Straight . . .<br />Into</b> . . .<br />My <b>heart</b> . . .</i>
</blockquote><br /><br /><b>
  <i>.... I'll let Will complete this wonderful piece, his piece, for his girl.</i>
</b><br /><br />------------------------------------------------------<br /><br />Readers, I'll say this much...do <u>not</u> miss this book.But all of you who have yet to read Slammed....do not read this before.<br /><br />This is not a stand-alone.<br /><br />All that said...<b>READ IT NOW!!!!</b><br /><br /><br />That's all for now Readers,<br /><br />Gooodbye.<br /><br />P.S. - <b>
  <i>My sweet was the <u>beautiful</u> ending.<br />My suck....was the <u>ending.</u></i>
</b><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" href="/user/show/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada">Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer424475543" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7872334547099802818"><br/><b> STARS REALISTIC SO NOT AND BACKWARDS, LOVELY, SWEET FOUR </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392780i/756172.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Yes, I am talking backwards, I know, I ROCK! LOL<br/><br/>Ok, I wanted to write a nice and sweet and romantic review but you guys already did that, you guys even wrote slam, how can you be so AWESOME??? What can I do now??? Ok, I am not gonna write slam, I seriously don’t want to show my super talents haha.<br/><br/>I loved this book, yes, I did so why am I not giving it 5 stars? Simple, you just need to keep reading my review to find out.<br/><br/> <blockquote>Yeah...<br/>This <b><i>girl</i></b>.<br/>M</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText7872334547099802818" style="display:none"><br><b> STARS REALISTIC SO NOT AND BACKWARDS, LOVELY, SWEET FOUR </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392780i/756172.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes, I am talking backwards, I know, I ROCK! LOL<br><br>Ok, I wanted to write a nice and sweet and romantic review but you guys already did that, you guys even wrote slam, how can you be so AWESOME??? What can I do now??? Ok, I am not gonna write slam, I seriously don’t want to show my super talents haha.<br><br>I loved this book, yes, I did so why am I not giving it 5 stars? Simple, you just need to keep reading my review to find out.<br><br> <blockquote>Yeah...<br>This <b><i>girl</i></b>.<br>My mother would have <b><i>loved</i></b> this girl.<br>Too bad she was just a <b><i>dream</i></b>.<br>
</blockquote><br><br>This Girl tells us the story of Will &amp; Lake, just as Slammed but this time Will is the one telling us their love story.<br><br>Will, you are soooo perfect that I had to roll my eyes so many times it hurt. Seriously. I mean, I like reading about perfect characters but sometimes authors don’t keep them real and that’s what I felt while reading this.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392780i/756173._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <blockquote> “Sometimes two people need to fall apart to realize how much they need to fall back together” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>Yeah, that’s the thing about Hoover, she knows how to write and how to make you feel because I highlighted the whole book, true story.<br><br>The thing is after Slammed and POR they are together, this is not a spoiler, this is something you know when you start this book. They are in their honeymoon and after a lot of “action” they are having a break (super rolling eyes) and Lake asks Will to tell her how he lived their story. So he starts…<br><br>And Lake is just adorable, as much as she was in Slammed &amp; POR.<br>Long story short, they meet each other because they’re neighbors and then BAM! Will is her teacher so they can’t be together. Tough shit!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> “I guess I’ll see you third period, Mr. Cooper”<br>I’d so much rather be her Will. </blockquote>
</b><br><br>What did I love the most about this book? The slam! I must say I love this series because I had never heard about slam before and I love it! Will new slams where just GREAT, not to mention the old ones that made me cry…<br><br><blockquote>Then this <b>girl</b>…<br>Holy hell, this <b>girl</b>…<br>
</blockquote><br><br>I also loved their <b>Suck &amp; Sweet</b> moments, I keep playing that with my friends. And <b>Would You Rather</b>!!! OMG, that’s soooo funny.<br><br>So, let’s play something… Would You Rather reading my ranting about this book or not? If you chose no, the review is over at this point. If you chose yes, keep reading. I swear I wasn’t going to say this but then I wouldn’t be honest and I need to be.<br><br>These are the things I didn’t like about the book:<br><br>*Will was way too sweet for me. I get that he’s the main character and main characters are always perfect but sometimes they’re not real.<br><br>*Their sex in the honeymoon. Not the sex per se but how many times did they have sex? She was a virgin, right??? Why do authors do that? We all have been virgins and we know you don’t want to have sex more than 10 times the first time you’re popping your cherry, right? That’s unbelievable and authors should know better. But well, that’s just my opinion<br><br>*They got married before having sex in 2013??? Are you kidding me??? Is this an American thing? Because that’s NOT happening in Europe and I very much doubt it’s happening over there. Why do authors think we are gonna love the MC more if he “respects” her until they’re married?<br> <br>Anyway, overall I loved this book but I cannot give it a 5 because I had some issues. Really hope you guys don’t want to kill me now but I wanted to be honest. <br><br>Let me say I loved being in his head, Will Cooper is a great book boyfriend, not real but a great one!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392780i/756174.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7872334547099802818" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_404433828" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/404433828" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/404433828?book_show_action=true">Aug 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews?shelf=2013">2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer404433828" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18409622994678086105"><b>Hi, my name is Mollie and I'm a objectum-sexual...</b><br/><br/><b>Object·o·phil·ia</b><br/><i>Noun</i><br/>1. Pronounced emotional and often romantic desire towards developing significant relationships with particular inanimate objects. Those individuals with this expressed preference may feel strong feelings of arousal, attraction, love, and commitment to certain items or structures of their fixation.<br/><br/>2. Belief that objects have souls, intelligence, feelings, and are able to communicate.<br/><br/>My objectphilic nature towards <i>This Girl</i> stem</span>
  <span id="freeText18409622994678086105" style="display:none"><b>Hi, my name is Mollie and I'm a objectum-sexual...</b><br /><br /><b>Object·o·phil·ia</b><br /><i>Noun</i><br />1. Pronounced emotional and often romantic desire towards developing significant relationships with particular inanimate objects. Those individuals with this expressed preference may feel strong feelings of arousal, attraction, love, and commitment to certain items or structures of their fixation.<br /><br />2. Belief that objects have souls, intelligence, feelings, and are able to communicate.<br /><br />My objectphilic nature towards <i>This Girl</i> stems from the fact I believe that this book without a doubt <i>does</i> have a soul. In fact, that could be said about <i>any</i> Colleen Hoover novel. <br /><br />Okay, so maybe objectophilia is a bit of an overkill, but it is completely safe to say that I have developed an intense fixation, a "pronounced emotional desire and strong feelings of love" for this amazing series. I believe that this book <i>can</i> communicate. It communicates straight to the heart and soul. <br /><br />Colleen Hoover did so much more than just retell a story. She created a fresh new approach to something that was already perfect. She perfected perfection and then perfected it again. She gave us a new story by telling us the old one. Retelling the past, but moving towards the future. You get two books in one. You get <i>Slammed</i> from Will's point of view, but you also get the continuation of Will and Layken's story after <i>Point of Retreat</i>. <br /><br />Colleen Hoover shoots talent from her fingers and emotion from her words. Everything she writes is flawless. <i>This Girl</i> is flawless. I can always count on everything from her books...everything. <i>This</i> is everything. I couldn't have asked for a better ending to a series that I never wanted to end. <br /><br />Colleen Hoover gives us a piece of her heart with every book she writes, every sentence...every word. You <i>will</i> love every word!<br /><br />Objectophiles unite!<br /><br />READ ON!<br /><br /><b><i>This Girl</i> BOOK TRAILER</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=1AY7XWGfnys">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=1AY7XW...</a><br /><br />More reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blogspot.com">http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blo...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="18409622994678086105" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText17159308275646688750" style="display:none">4.5 ★'s<br><br><blockquote>This girl got <b>schooled</b> by a boy who wasn't <i>thirty kinds of <b>mean</b>.</i> <br><br>This boy fell <b>hard</b> for this <b>beautiful</b> girl, Holy <b>hell</b>, this girl who's not a <b>dream</b> anymore. <br><br>This boy and this girl get to have their <b>final piece</b> of the puzzle.</blockquote><br><br>★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>My Will</u>
  </i>

  </i>
</b><br><br>Getting an epilogue!<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>My Suck:</u>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Getting an epilogue for the end of a series! :(<br><br><br>★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆<br><br>It was really great catching back up with Will and Lake. I sooo enjoyed them on their honeymoon. It was amazing to see them sooo happy but in a bittersweet sort of way. <br><br>You definitely won't understand this if you haven't read at least the first book in the series. I really wish there would have been more events retold especially more from <i>Point of Retreat</i> but I understand that you can only write so much. <br><br>If you've already read <i>Slammed</i> and <i>Point of Retreat</i>, you won't want to miss this. Some of the events from Will's POV are priceless.<br><br>♥ It wasn't just <b>carving pumpkins</b>, it was <b>butterflying</b> wonderful!! ♥<br><br>♥ I. And. <b>Love</b>. And. You. ♥ <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379790634i/539635.png" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ <br><br><br>Favorite quotes:<br><br>♥ "I was so in crush with you, Will."<br><br>♥ “Wife,” I say, staring straight into her eyes. “Think what you want, but there isn’t a single woman in this whole damn universe that I could ever love like I love you.”<br><br>♥ "I love you, Lake." I lean my forehead against hers. "You deserve to come first." <br><br>♥ “Wife? Are you sure you’re ready to not call retreat? Right now?” <br><br>She wraps her legs around me and pulls me closer. “I’m butterflying positive,” she says.<br><br><br>★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ The <b>butterflying</b> end ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★ ~ ☆ ~ ★<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17159308275646688750" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1152956571" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1152956571" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1152956571?book_show_action=true">Jan 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476746531" href="/book/show/17697452-this-girl">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1152956571" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5363338467960973240"><b> 4 Sweet stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “I want to be your soulmate, even if I don't believe in them.” </i> </b><br/><br/>Short review this time. <b> This Girl </b> begins with Lake and Will on their honeymoon.<br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/thisgirlhm.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420437699i/13225071.png' alt=' photo thisgirlhm.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Lake and Will are taking a, um, breather, and Will begins to tell Lake the story of how he met her. Before long it turns into his perspective of their entire story.<br/><br/>It's been so damn long since I first read Slammed, it was one of the first new adult type books I had ever read and there's a reason it's a classic. So reading this book</span>
  <span id="freeText5363338467960973240" style="display:none"><b> 4 Sweet stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> “I want to be your soulmate, even if I don't believe in them.” </i> </b><br><br>Short review this time. <b> This Girl </b> begins with Lake and Will on their honeymoon.<br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/thisgirlhm.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420437699i/13225071.png" alt=" photo thisgirlhm.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lake and Will are taking a, um, breather, and Will begins to tell Lake the story of how he met her. Before long it turns into his perspective of their entire story.<br><br>It's been so damn long since I first read Slammed, it was one of the first new adult type books I had ever read and there's a reason it's a classic. So reading this book was kind of like reading Slammed all over again, because I didn't actually remember much about Lake and Will after all this time. <br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/lakeandwill.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420437699i/13225072.png" alt=" photo lakeandwill.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I loved getting to see Will's side of things, of his struggle to maintain his integrity while his heart was telling him to do otherwise. The parts of Slammed where he seemed stoic or indifferent were explained. I had never thought of him as a jerk or butthead in the first book, and in this he proved he was a great guy.<br><br><b> <i> “She deserves to be kissed by someone who loves her. Someone who spends every waking moment trying to do everything right by her. Someone who would rather die than see her hurt. She doesn't deserve to be kissed by anyone other than me.” </i> </b><br><br>There's really not much more to say, the majority of us know Lake and Will's story, and for a retelling CoHo did an amazing job. I normally hate the same book/different point of view thing this genre tends to put out, but CoHo mixed it up and included a bunch of new in with the old.<br><br><b> <i> “You want to know my sweet? You. Always you.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/lakeandwillrain.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420437699i/13225073._SY540_.png" alt=" photo lakeandwillrain.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i> **small random: reading this made me really want a grilled cheese. I blame Coho for the random food craving** </i></span>
