    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_463793339" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/463793339" />
    <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday"><img alt="Ash Wednesday" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379043440p2/10484016.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/463793339?book_show_action=true">Nov 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ash Wednesday" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday">Ash Wednesday</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fans of Will and Layken's story</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=heartwarming">heartwarming</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=student-teacher">student-teacher</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer463793339" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7511951779253331728"><i>
  <b>3 STARS</b>
</i><br/><br/><b>
  <i>We're born into the world<br/>As just one small piece to the puzzle<br/>That makes up an entire life.<br/>It's up to us throughout our years,<br/>to find all the pieces that fit.<br/>The pieces that connect who we are<br/>To who we were<br/>To who we'll one day be.</i>
</b><br/><br/>No snazzy gifs or pictures, I feel bad enough writing this.<br/><br/>Before I get pitchforked and stoned to death I have to explain my love and faith in Colleen Hoover. I LOVE this woman. If you've read her blog posts, her books, her poetry, how can you not?! Serio</span>
  <span id="freeText7511951779253331728" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>3 STARS</b>
</i><br /><br /><b>
  <i>We're born into the world<br />As just one small piece to the puzzle<br />That makes up an entire life.<br />It's up to us throughout our years,<br />to find all the pieces that fit.<br />The pieces that connect who we are<br />To who we were<br />To who we'll one day be.</i>
</b><br /><br />No snazzy gifs or pictures, I feel bad enough writing this.<br /><br />Before I get pitchforked and stoned to death I have to explain my love and faith in Colleen Hoover. I LOVE this woman. If you've read her blog posts, her books, her poetry, how can you not?! Seriously. I love all her past work beyond 5-stars (I status-ed <i>Hopeless</i> to the ever living annoyance of my friends). She has this way of sneaking up on you ever so subtly, with well-paced charm and humor then Bam! you're crying over the magic purple hair clip (it still got me this time, btw). <br /><br />Just as a precaution, waterproof mascara or bust when it comes to Colleen Hoovering in public.<br /><br />Which was why when I heard that her next book was going to be Will's POV from <i>Slammed</i> I was quite a bit wary. I do not usually enjoy these alternate POVs because it feels a bit dangerous messing up with beloved characters.<b>Sometimes, it's what's unsaid that usually tugs the heart hardest</b>. I'm not sure if I want to know what Will was thinking while he performed that beautiful poem about oceans and lakes. But I figured if there's anyone who can prove me wrong, it's this author.<br /><br />What I took away from this book <b> is that <i>Slammed</i> isn't Will and Lake and the reasons that I fell head over heels about the book wasn't <u>solely</u> because of them</b>. It was what Julia and Eddie and Kel and Caulder made of them when they interacted with these characters. Connections I sorely missed in this 256-pages long of Will mooning over Layken and how much he wants to kiss her but can't. Telling the story in this manner felt like the story was just restricted to the two of them, and most of the time <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[except their fight about Taylor <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> when they pop up at the beginning of each chapter they just come across as making off-hand, unnecessary comments <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[("Gavin knew?" "You went out on a date?" and so on) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> they tend to get annoying. I feel if the story was told with Will having a conversation with anyone else other than Lake (maybe Kiersten or Kel), the variety and humor would've vastly improved the book.<br /><br />I loved the first chapter but after that, it was endless, lengthy soliloquies of Will's overwhelming love and raging desire over Lake (though I guess this is keeping up with his character, since he is a poet). Which was sweet, and I liked it for a while, but it just got too relentless for me to feel anything else but fatigue over that emotion (gasp! Did I just say that?). For a while I tried to alternate reading the scenes here and the equivalent scenes in <i>Slammed</i> but go too lazy and figured, this should stand on its own merits outside that book.<br /><br />This is probably the most un-Colleen Hoover book I've read (and I've read a few that try to emulate her) and save for the first chapter and the last 25%, Will just alienated me so much. The addition of the scenes with <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Taylor <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> was interesting at first because it led to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[that great scene at the hotel where Lake was baring her insecurities to him <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. But then, right at the scene in Slammed where Lake agrees to go out with Nick, we get a sneak peek at Will's thoughts while he bears witness to the conversation between Lake and Eddie. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>Lake could have at least had the decency to agree to a date when she's not standing five feet from me.</b>
</i><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[This after he went out on a date with Taylor, which he kept as a secret from Layken <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> until their honeymoon. I'm going to forget that ever went through this lovely boy's head because, seriously why are you asking me to hate you, Will?<br /><br />What I loved about this book are the ones that were already in <i>Slammed</i> (Layken's 'Schooled' poem still left me a bawling mess), the break up scene with Vaughn, the fact that I got to near-buddy read this with nearly everyone in my feed and <b>every damn scene Julia was in</b> right to that last, gutting star. I wish there were more Julia and Eddie scenes and less of Will wanting to be a coffee cup or Layken's knees and teeth (those last two were weird). I wish he'd had a life outside of Lake while still being in love with her. Because apparently, the moment he met her, the world ceased to exist. Literally.<br /><br />Don't be mistaken, I'd still recommend this to fans of Will and Layken. They had great moments together and the epilogue was wonderful. If this will make fans of <i>Slammed</i> as a whole (like me) happy as an addition to an already perfect duet of books, is a good point of discussion, I think. <br /><br />Right now, I am looking at Holder, with crazy nervous eyes.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7511951779253331728" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer423148396" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15102154815592067293"><b>And that’s how it’s done folks!<br/><br/>A masterpiece!</b><br/><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/><br/>The book was so perfect that it broke the star scale here.<br/><br/>BUT then...<br/>Then THIS BOOK<br/>Holy Hell, THIS BOOK ...<br/><br/><br/><i>“If I took every romantic poem, every book, every song, and every movie I've ever read, heard or seen and extracted the breathtaking moments, somehow bottling them up, they would pale in comparison to this moment.<br/><br/>This moment is incomparable.” </i><br/><br/><br/><b>*singing loudly and very poorly* <br/>"I'M SOOOOO EXCITED AND I JUST CAN'T HIDE IT!!!!!!!"</b><br/><br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392575ra/755691.gif' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><br/>I don</span>
  <span id="freeText15102154815592067293" style="display:none"><b>And that’s how it’s done folks!<br><br>A masterpiece!</b><br><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><br>The book was so perfect that it broke the star scale here.<br><br>BUT then...<br>Then THIS BOOK<br>Holy Hell, THIS BOOK ...<br><br><br><i>“If I took every romantic poem, every book, every song, and every movie I've ever read, heard or seen and extracted the breathtaking moments, somehow bottling them up, they would pale in comparison to this moment.<br><br>This moment is incomparable.” </i><br><br><br><b>*singing loudly and very poorly* <br>"I'M SOOOOO EXCITED AND I JUST CAN'T HIDE IT!!!!!!!"</b><br><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392575ra/755691.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>I don’t even think I can form a sentence worthy of what this series meant to me, so I won’t even try to write a “real” review. <br><br><b>And, So, the RANT begins:</b><br><br><br>The angels are singing, the trumpets are playing, and the fairytale princesses are abandoning their castles to head towards Will Cooper! I. AM. NOT. KIDDING.<br><br><br> <br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392575ra/755692.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>I never thought it would be possible to fall more in love with him but I really did. *sigh*<br>Will is just as swoon-worthy as ever. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392575ra/755693.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><i>Yes, I know. <br>We all love our bad boys but Will...Will is someone you would be proud to introduce to your Mom and Dad. </i><br><br> <br><br>He's not only good-looking but he truly has the biggest heart ever.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392575i/755694.jpg" width="400" height="550" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He's protective, sweet, responsible, talks about her "ugly shirt" AND writes poetry. I mean, come on, what's not to love about that.<br><br><br>I don’t see how any man can compete with this…<br><br> <b>"Out of all the reasons I can come up with for her to go, there is only one reason I can come up with for her to stay. I love her."<br><br><br>"She deserves to be kissed by someone who loves her. Someone who spends every waking moment trying to do everything right by her. Someone who would rather die than see her hurt. She doesn't deserve to be kissed by anyone other than me."<br><br><br><br>"I dreamt about this girl last night.<br>Wow. <i>This girl.</i><br>This girl completely shatters the window to my soul and crawls inside."</b> <br><br><br>See what I mean?<br>He is perfect.......in every stinkin’ way.<br><br>He had me swooning in my seat the entire time reading This Girl.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392575ra/755695.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>And OMG the love you can feel radiating off the pages between Will and Lake is <i>purely magical</i>.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392575i/755696.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They have suffered so much loss in their lives, so to see them finally in a beautiful place made my heart happy. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380390062i/751568.png" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The fact they are no longer retreating didn't hurt things either!*wink wink*<br><br>And the ending? The ending was so damn perfect that I have absolutely no words left.<br><br><b>“You, baby girl. You’re my final piece.”</b><br><br><br>Their story <i>slammed</i> our hearts and we are <b>seriously, deeply, madly, incredibly and undeniably</b> fell in <b>love</b> with it.<br><br><br>Now, I'm just sad it's over. I'm going to miss Will, Lake and the gang and the amazing slams. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392575i/755697.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>P.S: <i>My sweet is this book.<br>My suck is saying good bye to Will and Lake!</i></b></span>

  <span id="freeText8915654023034467310" style="display:none">A MILLION BUTTERFLYING STARS!!! I NEED MORE STARS !!!!!!! <br><br>Words cannot express how much I loved this book !!! Wills point of view was so captivating. How the story went back and forth from present to past. It was the best walk down memory lane. <br><br>The book opens up with The Honeymoon ❤ so from the get go I was in Swoon City.<br><br>" Sometimes two people need to fall apart to realize how much they need to fall back together."<br><br>" What was it like the first time you saw me ? " she asks. " What was it about me that made you want to ask me out? And tell me everything, even the bad thoughts." <br><br>I laugh. " There weren't any bad thoughts. Naughty thoughts, maybe. But not bad."<br><br>She grins. "Well tell me those, too."<br>The re telling of their story was so peaceful and beautiful. Like a butterfly kissing a Lake ❤<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403241i/784434._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The best part of falling in love with Will and Lake's story was .....FALLING IN LOVE AGAIN....             Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7373882-angela?shelf=owned-physical">owned-physical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7373882-angela?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7373882-angela?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7373882-angela?shelf=books-library-owns">books-library-owns</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7373882-angela?shelf=2013-april">2013-april</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer410260016" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4710726028497027382">I have mixed feeling about this. It's not quite what I expected it to be. I found it much too similar to <i>Slammed</i>. There was nothing exciting, because I already knew what's coming up. As much as I loved <i>Slammed</i>, <i>This Girl</i> was just boring. I actually skimmed some parts because it's too repetitive. Where is the new material??</span>

          </span>
        </div>

Still, he can’t resist his wife’s pleas and so he begins to untangle his side of the story, revealing for the first time his most intimate feelings and thoughts, retelling both the good and bad moments, and sharing a few shocking confessions of his own from the time when they first met.<br><br>In This Girl, Will tells the story of their complicated relationship from his point of view. <div id="review_1485179348" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1485179348" />
    <a title="Jiana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana"><img alt="Jiana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540380229p2/10502567.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1485179348?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jiana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jiana" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana">Jiana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476746531" href="/book/show/17697452-this-girl">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1485179348" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9038967303869628962"><b>2.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Okay, look. Colleen Hoover is one of my all-time favorite authors. Four of her books are on my favorites shelf and I've never rated a book of hers below 4 stars before I read Point of Retreat in December 2016. Point of Retreat, book 2 in the Slammed trilogy, was a 2 star read. Look like this book has joined it, too. However, I did really enjoy book 1, Slammed, which I read around a year and a half ago. Probably if I had read it now, I wouldn't enjoy it as much.<br/><br/><i>
  <blockquote>“You, baby girl. You’re</blockquote></i></span>
  <span id="freeText9038967303869628962" style="display:none"><b>2.5 stars</b><br /><br />Okay, look. Colleen Hoover is one of my all-time favorite authors. Four of her books are on my favorites shelf and I've never rated a book of hers below 4 stars before I read Point of Retreat in December 2016. Point of Retreat, book 2 in the Slammed trilogy, was a 2 star read. Look like this book has joined it, too. However, I did really enjoy book 1, Slammed, which I read around a year and a half ago. Probably if I had read it now, I wouldn't enjoy it as much.<br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>“You, baby girl. You’re my final piece.”</blockquote>
</i><br /><br />I'm well aware this is one of CoHo's earliest works, so maybe that's why I didn't enjoy it. CoHo has matured as a writer <b>so much</b> since then. I usually go easy on debut books, but this isn't a debut so. <br /><br />Anyway, in Point of Retreat, I hated both Will and Layken. They were a childish couple. This Girl is Slammed in Will's POV; it's actually Will telling Layken during their honeymoon all his thoughts and feelings during the events of Slammed. I hoped I'd enjoy it because I enjoyed Slammed, but nah. I don't like Will, so I didn't really care about this thoughts. So basically, the book alternates between the present and the past. As Will told the story again, I realized how bad their story actually is, hence why I'm 99% if I reread Slammed, I'd hate it too. Will and Layken are <i>super</i> annoying. Annoying, cringey, and immature. During the present events? Still immature. Still cringey. Not cute. <br /><br /><b>The only thing I loved: the epilogue.</b><br /><br />That is all. At least I'm done with the trilogy! Now, I'll be painfully waiting for CoHo's next book!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9038967303869628962" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText10350416997791466276" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Check totallybooked for a teaser from THIS GIRL and a chance to win an Ebook copy and a signed Paperback Copy of This Girl</i>
</b><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://totallybookedblog.com/2013/04/27/this-girl-by-colleen-hoover-review-teaser-and-signed-paperback-and-ebook-giveaway/">http://totallybookedblog.com/2013/04/...</a><br /><br />Our thoughts by Jenny &amp; Gitte<br /><br />This is a review with a difference so we hope you’ll bear with us.<br /><br />We were going to discuss the contents of this book but scrapped that idea because…well, it’s Colleen Hoover so you know it’s well written. Most of you already know Will and Layken and all the other characters from the Slammed Series (if you don’t then pick this series up now!) so you know you’re going to love them and you know from this authors writing style that this book is going to have heart….and lots of it.<br /><br />And let’s face it, we know you guys would rather read the book for yourselves than have us tell you about it.<br /><br />So instead, we’re going to talk about what this book meant to us.<br /><br />We loved Slammed and Point of Retreat with all our hearts. What we didn’t realise until reading This Girl was how much we genuinely missed all these characters.<br /><br />Sure, we knew what an impact these characters had had on us and how much they had become a part of our lives but being reunited with them again after a year was like meeting up with old friends and every minute spent in This Girl took us back to that moment when we read Slammed and Point of Retreat. You know the one? That “moment” we refer to at TB as “Book Love”. That special feeling you get when you’ve just experienced a story so beautiful, characters so enchanting and writing so magical that you feel it deep down in your bones and you know, without a doubt, it’s going to stay with you forever.<br /><br />There are moments in life you can recall in a heartbeat. The ones where you’re transported back in time to a moment you want to relive because it left a mark on you. It made you happy and it brought warmth to your soul. It was so special you wanted to tuck it away in your heart and bring it out at a time when you needed to put that smile back on your face.<br /><br />Well, the Slammed Series was that for us. We can recall every moment, every second of how we felt and the warm feeling those books brought to us when we were reading them. They will stay with us for life, of that we’re sure.<br /><br />So, knowing we were going back to that was always going to feel special.<br /><br />But we won’t lie to you. There was a certain amount of trepidation going into this for us. Was this going to simply be a retelling of Slammed? Was it just Slammed told from Will’s POV? Were we going to get bored and skim? After all, we know the story of Slammed already and we had previously heard Will’s voice in Point of Retreat so we knew what to expect from him. Yes readers, we were worried. We wanted to love it, but dreaded the possibility that maybe we wouldn’t.<br /><br />We’re delighted to say all our fears were allayed about one chapter in. We were back! That same warm, wonderful feeling was back and we were once again basking in book love glow!<br /><br />First off, we’re not going to refer to This Girl as “Slammed from Will’s POV” because for us that is too simple a term for how wonderful and beautiful this book was. We consider This Girl to be an “extension” of the series. A must have for fans of Slammed and Point of Retreat. It really does offer THAT much!<br /><br />Sure, technically it is Slammed told by Will but readers it is so, so much more. We get new perspectives, new moments, new emotions and completely new scenes both current and past. This story is told in a back and forth composition which is so perfectly executed, so precisely timed that the reader is taken on a journey through Will’s eyes that will leave you spellbound in its beauty and telling. The epilogue is something book lovers dream about and being that we are both readers first and reviewer/bloggers second, we can tell you that this book completely captivated us and it’s the thing book memories are made of.<br /><br />So, how much did we love This Girl? Let us tell you this. Ask us in a year…hell…no! Ask us in five years what we were doing at the time and how we felt whilst reading This Girl and we know, with absolute certainty that we’ll be able to tell you because this book left a mark on us to the point where we will be able to recall every emotion and every minute of how we felt whilst immersed in this story. Throw listening to I And Love And You by the Avett Brothers into the mix and we’ll be right back to April 2013 in the blink of an eye.<br /><br />Colleen Hoover has the ability to write about moments and turn them into memories.<br /><br />So, don’t hesitate. Pick it up. Devour it, and then be sure to share that memory with someone else, because after all, memories are better when shared.<br /><br /> </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4141938505032361612"><b>★★★★★5 Million Stars!!!! ★★★★★<br/>I don't quite know how to express the depth of my love for this book...and this series...and Will-freaking-Cooper!!!!!</b><br/><br/><b>SENSATIONAL!!!!</b><br/>No words I can come up with can fully express how much I loved this book and this series. Colleen Hoover has created a beautiful story with Will and Layken and told it so effortlessly. It will forever hold a place in my most favorite books <b>EVER!!!!!</b> <br/><br/>Before you read further...if you haven't read <b>Slammed or Point of Retreat, stop and GO </b></span>
  <span id="freeText4141938505032361612" style="display:none"><b>★★★★★5 Million Stars!!!! ★★★★★<br>I don't quite know how to express the depth of my love for this book...and this series...and Will-freaking-Cooper!!!!!</b><br><br><b>SENSATIONAL!!!!</b><br>No words I can come up with can fully express how much I loved this book and this series. Colleen Hoover has created a beautiful story with Will and Layken and told it so effortlessly. It will forever hold a place in my most favorite books <b>EVER!!!!!</b> <br><br>Before you read further...if you haven't read <b>Slammed or Point of Retreat, stop and GO READ THEM RIGHT NOW!!!</b><br><br>This story begins where Point of Retreat left off, with the couple on their honeymoon. Which was unfortunately only a weekend off alone together. But it was a perfect conclusion to the year of up’s and downs they encountered with their relationship and with Layken’s mother’s illness. It was a perfect ending for this series and a perfect beginning for them. <br><br>The story is told from Will Cooper’s POV. And I cannot stress enough how swoony it was to live in that man’s head!!! I will repeat what I’ve read from a friend’s review…that Colleen Hoover has very likely created the <b>perfect</b> man!!!! I cannot think of one negative thing to say about Will Cooper…. except that maybe he is just too perfect!!!!!<br><br>In this book, Will is recounting his feelings and experiences to Lake on their honeymoon; his feelings about his parents and their death, his breakup with Vaughn, as well as their meeting, and all of the times they shared together. Lake was finally getting to hear his side of the story. There were secrets revealed, and many feelings divulged that shed new light on their relationship and their love for each other. I also loved sharing a bit of the honeymoon moments with them as well (even though I wished it were me!!!).<br><br>To me, this was the perfect epilogue for the Slammed Series. Such an incredibly sweet, and at times, very sad love story between two young adults left behind after their parents’ deaths. They were both left to take care of younger siblings, and become parents themselves long before they should have. And their history, with their instant chemistry, the tragedy of their unknown circumstance, Will’s responsibilities and their determination to stay <s>apart</s> together all while dealing with <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the tragedy of Layken’s mother’s illness and death, <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> made for such a truly compelling read. <br><br>I don’t want to mention too many details of the story, but I have to say that what brought it all together for me, what catapulted this book into the stratosphere for me was the <b>realness</b> and <b>beauty</b> of all of the characters. I loved each and every one of them, (<i>excluding Vaughn</i>). The dialogue was just amazing, the kids… Kel and Caulder were <b>butterflying perfect</b>, and the <b>poetry</b> my God, the <b>POETRY was BRILLANT</b>. <br><br>Even the epilogue was perfect… I am speechless…<br><br><b>BEAUTIFUL JOB COLLEEN!!!!! 5 MILLION STARS!!!!!!!!!!!</b><br><br>Here are my pics for Will and Layken!!<br><br><b>Will Cooper<br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/MarcoDapper125.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909056i/3177398._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo MarcoDapper125.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Layken Cohen Cooper</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/Laken.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_396014364" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/396014364" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/396014364?book_show_action=true">Aug 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer396014364" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16442398684957291172"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388326i/748716.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>After fabulous <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13372690.Slammed__Slammed___1_' title='Slammed (Slammed, #1) by Colleen Hoover' rel='nofollow noopener'>Slammed</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13496084.Point_of_Retreat__Slammed___2_' title='Point of Retreat (Slammed, #2) by Colleen Hoover' rel='nofollow noopener'>Point of Retreat</a> this was a must read for me! I was looking forward to spending some more time with Will, Layken and their family and I got exactly what I had expected. I laughed, I cried, I swooned. This Girl was superb conclusion to this amazing series and I loved it all!</b><br/>My Will and Lake:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388326i/748717.jpg' width='250' height='380' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388326i/748718.jpg' width='250' height='380' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>SPOILER-FREE REVIEW<br/>I am going to be short and sweet. There are no words to describe how perfect Will's and Lake's story is. You just have to experience it yourself. All those amazing</span>
  <span id="freeText16442398684957291172" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388326i/748716.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>After fabulous <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13372690.Slammed__Slammed___1_" title="Slammed (Slammed, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Slammed</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13496084.Point_of_Retreat__Slammed___2_" title="Point of Retreat (Slammed, #2) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Point of Retreat</a> this was a must read for me! I was looking forward to spending some more time with Will, Layken and their family and I got exactly what I had expected. I laughed, I cried, I swooned. This Girl was superb conclusion to this amazing series and I loved it all!</b><br>My Will and Lake:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388326i/748717.jpg" width="250" height="380" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388326i/748718.jpg" width="250" height="380" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>SPOILER-FREE REVIEW<br>I am going to be short and sweet. There are no words to describe how perfect Will's and Lake's story is. You just have to experience it yourself. All those amazing reviews and ratings of Slammed series talk for themselves and This Girl is no exception. This Girl reminded me of watching bonus materials on DVD of my favourite movie - you know what is about to happen, you know how it is going to end but you just cannot get enough and you want more, you want deeper insight into the story and characters. I simply loved it and was really glad that it didn't feel repetitive.<br><br>It was absolutely fantastic to relive one of my all time favourite stories from Will's POV. He is great man, brother, boyfriend... And he is also believable character. I loved him in previous books and my love for him even grew in this book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388326i/748719.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I admire Colleen Hoover for creating such adorable and lovable characters who will always have a special place in my heart and on my bookshelf. Will, Lake, Coulder, Kel... I love them all and I am sure I will be coming back to their story.<br><br>Anyway, I cannot write much without giving spoilers. All I can say is that if you haven't read this series yet, do so now. You won't regret it. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13372690.Slammed__Slammed___1_" title="Slammed (Slammed, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Slammed</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13496084.Point_of_Retreat__Slammed___2_" title="Point of Retreat (Slammed, #2) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Point of Retreat</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15784909.This_Girl__Slammed___3_" title="This Girl (Slammed, #3) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">This Girl</a> are the best you can get when it comes to YA/NA contemporary romance. Freash ideas, unforgettable story, great writing. It is all there. You won't be able to put it down. And when you finish it, you will never forget this powerful and emotional story!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388326i/748720.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16442398684957291172" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_984952185" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/984952185" />
    <a title="Lazaros" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22313662-lazaros"><img alt="Lazaros" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578697302p2/22313662.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/984952185?book_show_action=true">Jul 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lazaros" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lazaros" href="/user/show/22313662-lazaros">Lazaros</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">romantics</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22313662-lazaros?shelf=tear-jerkers">tear-jerkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22313662-lazaros?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22313662-lazaros?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22313662-lazaros?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer984952185" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1741736251127843614"><b>Wow. Holy shit. This was all kinds of perfection. It was a heart-stopping read.</b> I loved the bejebus out of it.<br/><br/>I just can't stomach that there are people out there who might never find someone who makes them feel like Will makes Layken feel and vice versa. It should be considered a crime not to have someone to love and have them love you back so intensely. Luckily, I'm one of those people who've already found their love of their life and I really can confirm that this kind love is not only found </span>
  <span id="freeText1741736251127843614" style="display:none"><b>Wow. Holy shit. This was all kinds of perfection. It was a heart-stopping read.</b> I loved the bejebus out of it.<br /><br />I just can't stomach that there are people out there who might never find someone who makes them feel like Will makes Layken feel and vice versa. It should be considered a crime not to have someone to love and have them love you back so intensely. Luckily, I'm one of those people who've already found their love of their life and I really can confirm that this kind love is not only found in books. I hope you believe me and when you find this girl or boy who makes you feel special, who believes in you, who accepts for who you are, trusts you and love you and you can feel all those things when you look at them in the eyes, then don't ever butterflying let them get away. Fight with tooth and nail to make them see that what you have is worth all the oxygen you're breathing.<br /><br />This love Layken and Will have is every kind of truthful. I love that about this series. It's the best realistic fiction, romance series I've ever read for two reasons. It's really realistic and not out-of-this-world and the characters are deep, not perfect but deep. They all make mistakes and they all learn out of them but they never give up, they just get one foot up and they stand up and fight for what they've got and never stop believing in themselves and the people they love. There is so much love in these books. So much love. All kinds of love. Friendly love, family love, romantic love. It's a unique story and what makes it even more fun to read is the fact that there are twists, so, you never get bored reading about these lovable characters.<br /><br />I gave this 5 stars because it's practically the sweetest thing I've ever read. It was a mix of the first book with Layken and Will's honeymoon. Will would tell her what they lived through the first book from his own point of view and then they were together on their honeymoon laughing and crying because most of them were bittersweet memories that they managed to get past. And now they are going to live happily ever after.<br /><br />I loved Will's poem (his final piece) in the end of the book and there couldn't have been a more ideal way to bring this series to its end. Read the following excerpt on your own accord. Spoilers ahead.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <b>We're born into the world<br />As just one small piece to the puzzle<br />That makes up an entire life.<br />It's up to us throughout our years,<br />to find all of our pieces that fit.<br />The pieces that connect who we are<br />To who we were<br />To who we'll one day be.<br />Sometimes pieces will almost fit.<br />They'll feel right.<br />We'll carry them around for a while,<br />Hoping they'll conform to our puzzle.<br />But they won't.<br />We'll eventually have to let them go.<br />To find the puzzle that is their home.<br />Sometimes pieces won't fit at all.<br />No matter how much we want them to.<br />We'll shove them.<br />We'll bend them.<br />We'll break them.<br />But what isn't meant to be,<br />won't be.<br />Those are the hardest pieces of all to accept.<br />The pieces of our puzzle<br />That just don't belong.<br />But occasionally...<br />Not very often at all,<br />If we're lucky,<br />If we pay enough attention,<br />We'll find a <br />perfect match.<br />The pieces of the puzzle that slide right in<br />The pieces that hug the contours of our own pieces.<br />The pieces that lock to us.<br />The pices that we lock to.<br />The pieces that fit so well, we can't tell where our piece begins<br />And that piece ends/<br />Those pieces we call<br />Friends.<br />True loves.<br />Dreams.<br />Passions.<br />Belifs.<br />Talents.<br />They're all the pieces that complete our puzzles.<br />They line the edges,<br />Frame the corners,<br />Those pieces are the pieces that makes us who we are.<br />Who we were.<br />Who we'll one day be.<br />Up until today,<br />When I looked at my own puzzle,<br />I would see a finished piece/<br />I had the edges lined,<br />The corners framed,<br />The cented filled.<br />It felt like it was complete.<br />All the pieces therespan.<br />I had everything I wanted.<br />Everything I need.<br />Everything I dreamt of.<br />But up until today,<br />I realized I had collected all <br />but one piece.<br />The most vital piece.<br />The piece that completes the picture.<br />The piece that completes my whole life.<br />I held this girl in my arms<br />She wrapped her tiny fingers around mine.<br />It was then that I realized<br />She was the fusion.<br />The glue.<br />The cement that bound all my pieces together.<br />The piece that seals my puzzle.<br />The piece that completes my life.<br />The element that makes me who I am.<br />Who I was.<br />Who I'll one day be.<br />You, baby girl.<br />You're my final piece.</b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

</a><br><br><br><i>The final chapter of Will and Lake. I LOVED "This Girl" so, so much! Will was absofreakinglutely <b>PERFECT, AMAZING, WONDERFUL, SWEET, LOYAL, AWESOME, FABULOUS, KIND, PROTECTIVE, and LOVING</b>...I could go on and on...I'm in CRUSH :)</i><br><b>My sweet</b>: reading this book *sigh*<br><b>My suck:</b> the book series is over *sigh*<br><br><br>“I got schooled this year<br><b>by<br>a<br>boy.</b><br><br>A boy that I'm <b>seriously, deeply, madly, incredibly, and undeniably in love</b> with.<br>And he taught me the most important thing of <b>all</b>...<br><br>To put the <b>emphasis</b><br>On <b>life.”</b><br><br><br><b>My WILL</b><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/zac%20efron" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386513i/746026.jpg" alt="zac efron photo: zac efron zac-efron.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>"There are over thirty different meanings and substitutions for the word <i>MEAN</i><br><b>Jackass, jerk, cruel, dickhead, unkind, harsh, wicked, hateful, heartless, vicious, virulent, unrelenting, tyrannical, malevolent, atrotious, bastard, barbarous, bitter, brutal, callous, degenerate, brutish, depraved, evil, fierce, hard, implacable, rancorous, pernicious, inhumane, monstrous, merciless, inexorable. And my personal favorite...</b><i>ASSHOLE.</i><br><br><br><b>My LAKE</b><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/Britt%20robertson" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386513i/746027.jpg" alt="Britt robertson photo: Kate britt-robertson-7863.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>"Layken Cooper, I love you. I've loved you since the second I laid eyes on you and I haven't stopped loving you for a second since."</b><br><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/I%20butterfly%20you" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386513ra/746028.gif" alt="I butterfly you photo: I love you Butterfly.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/holding%20hands" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386513i/746029.jpg" alt="holding hands photo: holding-hands holding-hands.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>"I think back to that day. The day that I fell for my wife."</b><br><br><b>"I just want to know everything about you. I've already got your future, now I want to get to know your past."</b><br><br><br>I used to <i>love</i> the ocean.<br><i>Everything</i> about her.<br>Her coral <i>reefs,</i> her <i>whitecaps,</i> her roaring <br><i>waves,</i> the<br>rocks they <i>lap,</i> her <i>pirate</i> legends and<br><i>mermaid</i> tails,<br>Treasures <i>lost</i> and <i>treasures</i> held...<br>And ALL<br>Of her <i>fish</i><br>In the <i>sea.</i><br>Yes, I used to <i>love</i> the ocean,<br><i>Everything</i> about her.<br>The way she would <i>sing</i> me to <i>sleep</i> as I <i>lay</i><br>in my bed<br>then <i>wake</i> me with a <i>force</i><br>That I <i>soon</i> came to <i>dread.</i><br>her <i>fables,</i> her lies, her <i>misleading</i> eyes,<br>I'd drain her <i>dry</i><br>If I <i>cared</i> enough to.<br>I used to <i>love</i> the ocean,<br><i>Everything</i> about her.<br>Her coral <i>reefs,</i> her <i>whitecaps,</i> her roaring <br><i>waves,</i> the<br>rocks they <i>lap,</i> her <i>pirate</i> legends, and<br><i>mermaid</i> tails,<br>treasures <i>lost</i> and treasures <i>held.</i><br>And ALL<br>Of her <i>fish</i><br>In the <i>sea.</i><br>Well, if you've ever tried <i>navigating</i> your<br><i>sailboat</i><br>through the stormy <i>seas,</i> you would <i>realize</i><br>that<br>her <i>whitecaps</i> are your <i>enemies.</i> If you've<br>ever tried<br><i>swimming ashore</i> when your leg gets a <i>cramp</i><br>and you had a <i>huge meal</i> of <i>In-n-Out</i><br>burgers that's<br><i>weighing</i> you down, and her <i>roaring waves</i><br>are<br>knocking the <i>wind,</i> out of you, filling your<br><i>lungs</i> with<br><i>water</i> as you <i>flail</i> your arms, trying to get<br><i>someone's</i><br>attention, but your friends<br>just <br>wave<br>back at you?<br>And if you've ever grown up with dreams<br>in your head<br>about life, and how one of these days you<br>would pirate<br>your own ship and have your own crew<br>and that all of <br>the mermaids<br>would love<br>only<br>you?<br>Well, you would realize...<br>Like I eventually realized...<br>That all the <i>good</i> things about her?<br>All the <i>beautiful?</i><br>It's not <i>real.</i><br>It's <i>fake.</i><br>So <b>keep</b> your <b>ocean,</b> <br><b>I'll</b> take the <b>Lake.</b><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/couples%20in%20love" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386513i/746030.jpg" alt="couples in love photo: couples couples.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>"You're the greatest thing that's ever happened to my life."<br>"I love you, Will Cooper, and I love you, Layken Cooper."<br><br>"THIS GIRL completely shatters the window to my soul and crawls inside."</b><br><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/puzzle%20pieces" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386513i/746031._SX540_.jpg" alt="puzzle pieces photo: puzzle-pieces puzzle-pieces.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>She was the <b>fusion.</b><br>The <b>glue</b><br>The <b>cement</b> that <b>bound</b> all my pieces<br>together.<br>The piece that seals my <b>puzzle.</b><br>The piece that completes my <b>life.<br>The element that makes me who <b>I am.</b><br>Who I was.<br>Who I'll <i>one day be.</i><br><i>You,</i> baby girl.<br><i>You're</i> my <i>final piece.</i></b></span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_15745950'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15745950-walking-disaster"><img alt="Walking Disaster (Beautiful, #2)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1352338368l/15745950._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('fSzBuApTU7vvtkU4slhWEyyDZ7oCLhcZaf+MPxeBBW5HCqhqsQ2a00id8VlFrVzM+tyAcsyjmX4ygcqO2sL39A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('JyLqRfwwneY/bWQzImDo0nB1AAbAB9E0BXsC2pLE8aUdBIOXR25UjphG0FLVleINpirnzg6KX1NeBURrX4cDPw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
</div>

<div class='navButtonArrow sliderArrowPrev'></div>
</div>
